Proclamation to All Citizens

(London) Sir Wollaston, Lord Chamberlain of the Royal Household, read the proclamation of the accession of the new King George VI from the balcony of St. James's Palace this afternoon. The ceremony was solemn and followed tradition. The crowd in front of the palace was immense, listening intently. The new monarch, along with Queen Mary and other members of the royal family, appeared on the balcony of nearby Marlborough House. The people cheered and paid their respects upon seeing them. Afterwards, Sir Wollaston went to three other locations, including Trafalgar Square, to read the proclamation. The weather today was cold and drizzly, quite different from the clear weather when the abdicated King ascended the throne in January of this year. The enthusiasm was also less than that of the 25th anniversary of the coronation of the late King George V in June of last year, but the people's sincere loyalty to the new monarch was the same. This could be seen in the collective cry of "God save the King" by the entire audience after the proclamation was read. The new King's proclamation reads as follows:

"In accordance with the King's Abdication Act of December 10, His Majesty King Edward VIII has declared that he and his descendants renounce the throne with firm and irrevocable intention. Therefore, the Abdication Act has now taken effect. The throne of the United Kingdom of Great Britain and Ireland, and the overseas dominions belonging to His Majesty the former King, shall, in accordance with the only rightful path, be taken by His Royal Highness Prince Albert Frederick Arthur George. We, the leaders of the church and state, together with the prominent ministers of His Majesty the former King's Privy Council, the Lord Mayor of London, and the gentry and citizens, hereby proclaim, with one heart and one voice, in the presence of all, that His Royal Highness Prince Albert Frederick Arthur George, by the grace of God, is established as the King of the United Kingdom of Great Britain and Ireland and the overseas dominions, Emperor of India, and Defender of the Faith. We solemnly pledge our enduring loyalty and affection, and earnestly pray to God to protect the King and Queen in governing our country. May God bless George VI and grant him health, happiness, and a long life to reign over us. Issued at St. James's Palace on December 20, 1936. God save the King." (Havas dispatch, 12th)

Address to the Army, Navy, and Air Force

(London) In accordance with the constitution, the British King, after ascending the throne, also assumes the position of Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force. The address to the Navy mentions that he and his father, the late Emperor, had received naval training in their early years and that he had witnessed the great achievements of the soldiers in maintaining the traditions of the British Navy during the greatest naval battle of the new era at Jutland. He said that he intended to maintain the closest possible contact with all officers and soldiers of the entire Navy of the Empire. The address to the Army assured the soldiers that he would prioritize their well-being and mentioned that he had been appointed a Major General in the Army four years ago. After associating with the Army, he was even more impressed by their bravery, seriousness, and dedication to their difficult duties. He concluded by saying that the task before him was very arduous, but he knew that all officers and soldiers of the entire Army of the Empire would express their loyalty to lighten his heavy burden. The address to the Air Force stated that he had served as a junior officer in the Air Force in 1918, after serving in the Independent Air Force in France, and that he had always regarded this as a happy part of his life. In the future, he would maintain a close relationship with the Air Force. As an Air Marshal, he was pleased to see that after the rapid expansion of the Air Force, its responsibilities were no less than those of the Army. He hoped that the Air Force of the Empire would maintain its achievements. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

Mediation of Spanish Conflict - Germany, Italy, and Portugal Refuse - Replies Delivered to British and French Governments - League of Nations Council Passes Resolution - Appeals to All Countries to Strictly Observe Neutrality 42

(Geneva) The League of Nations Council continued its public meeting at 6:00 PM and unanimously passed a resolution on the Spanish issue. The main points of its content are as follows:

(1) Recognizing that the situation in Spain is sufficient to affect international relations and may even threaten peace, therefore, all countries must strictly observe the principle of non-intervention in the internal affairs of other countries.

(2) Suggesting to the member states of the League of Nations attending the Non-Intervention Method Adjustment Committee to make the greatest efforts to quickly implement an effective monitoring system.

(3) Expressing sympathy for the British and French governments' proposal to mediate the Spanish civil war.

The last paragraph of the resolution suggests that countries cooperate to humanize the Spanish civil war and acknowledges that, in the future, after the end of the civil war, countries have a special need to assist Spain's domestic construction. The Council has authorized League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol to direct the League of Nations technical agencies to provide assistance when such assistance is necessary. When the resolution was submitted for debate, Spanish Foreign Minister Del Valle declared that he could accept the section of the resolution on the humanization of the Spanish civil war, but this kind of action should be initiated by the Spanish government and accepted by the League of Nations. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

Tokyo Correspondence: A Caricature of Japan's Military Industry Capital at the Present Stage (Part 2) 43

— Nagumo

Let's take another look at the most important types of goods imported into Japan, listing the eight most vital:

Wheat, beans, crude and heavy oil, cotton, wool, iron, machinery, timber.

Roughly eighty to ninety percent of imports are raw materials, with a small portion being semi-finished products. While wheat is imported, wheat flour is exported. Large quantities of cotton and wool are imported, and correspondingly large quantities of cotton cloth and woolen fabrics are exported. Only iron, and crude and heavy oil, are used to develop Japan's military industries.

However, no matter how much is imported, it always feels insufficient. The arms race will not stop until capitalism is destroyed, and all countries are the same. But the shortage of raw materials worries these ambitious individuals.

The United States is a major mineral-producing country, but due to shortages and competition, mineral prices are also rising there. This is a cause of great hardship for Japan, which desperately needs to import minerals. Let's examine this further from the perspective of rising prices:

Needless to say, iron is fundamental to the existence of all industries. In 1935, Japan's iron production reached 3.5 million tons, which could be said to barely meet domestic needs. However, it was still necessary to import iron ore, as Japan's domestic ore production was very small. Although there were mines, the amount extracted was also meager. Without the import of ore, iron could not be produced. Therefore, imports in 1935 reached 3.3 million tons. Even pig iron and scrap iron, used as raw materials for steel, had to be imported in large quantities. In 1935, pig iron imports reached one million tons and scrap iron 1.7 million tons. Compared to 1934, pig iron imports increased by 60 percent, and scrap iron by 20 percent. While imports increased, iron prices also soared. During Mussolini's invasion of Abyssinia, the price of iron for general use was 47.5 yuan per ton, and for steelmaking, it was 46.5 yuan. But recently (October -), the prices of both types of iron mentioned above have risen to 49 yuan. An increase of more than two yuan per ton, which, based on a demand of 3 million tons, would result in an additional cost of more than 6 million yuan. This can also be said to be one of the fundamental reasons for the increased burden (increased taxes) on the Japanese public today.

Most of the scrap iron is imported from the United States, but as the demand in the United States is also increasing, and because this is a raw material for the military industry, the "Export Prohibition Act" may be passed under certain circumstances – this further forces prices up. Currently, in Japan, one ton of high-quality iron is worth 60 yuan, an increase of nearly 20 yuan compared to last autumn.

It can be seen that "national iron production" and "trade control" are necessary cries. The fate of the Longyan Iron Mine in North China is being revived primarily under the current state of iron shortage.

Next is electrical copper, which is also very important. Before the European War, Japan's electrical copper was not only sufficient but also exported. However, due to competition with the United States and rapidly expanding needs, it has now become an importer of electrical copper. In the table above, we see that copper imports are also increasing year by year. In 1933, copper imports amounted to 9.6 million yuan. In 1934, it increased to 28.4 million yuan, a threefold increase. In 1935, it increased further, with imports totaling 37.9 million yuan. Because countries are all engaged in intense preparations for war, the need for copper has increased even more. Copper is soft and essential for metal alloys, and copper is the primary component of electrical wires.

Next is tin. Tin is very useful for plating iron sheets with gold and for metal alloys. World production is not very large, but demand is increasing, so market prices are also soaring.

Next are lead and zinc. Lead can be used to make lead pipes and lead chambers for manufacturing sulfuric acid without further refinement. As an alloy, it can be used to create storage batteries and printing type. It can also be used as a compound in pigments. It has a wide range of uses. But Japan must also import it. In 1933, 12 million yuan worth of lead was imported. In 1934, 17.9 million yuan was imported, and in 1935, it was 20.5 million yuan, also increasing year by year, but the rate of increase is not as large as that of iron and copper.

Zinc is used for plating iron sheets and in other chemical industrial products. Japan also has a considerable amount of domestic production, but it still inevitably imports zinc ore every year. However, this type of import is not large, averaging just over one million yuan per year. Market prices are, of course, also rising. The main lead-producing countries are the United States, Mexico, and Canada, but they are far from Japan, so it is best to purchase more to prepare for emergencies. This August, when lead prices were low, 100 kilograms were worth 36.6 yuan, but now it has risen to 39.8 yuan. Zinc has also risen from 35 yuan to 39 yuan.

The soaring prices of general military raw materials fully illustrate the preparations for war. And Japan is a first-class active participant.

Generally speaking, since the world economic crisis that originated in 1930, the world production index has not yet reached the level of 1929. Even the so-called "economic recovery" is only a "lame economic recovery." There is no doubt that world capitalism is suffering from a general chronic paralysis. But it is also a fact that Japan is a relatively prosperous country. Because Japan's national fortune, as the Japanese military says, "has progressed," and has progressed to the point where the current political institutions cannot adapt. In fact, Japan's foreign trade this year has declined compared to last year. The so-called economic recovery is actually an artificial economic recovery driven by the expansion of the military industry!

But when it comes to the raw materials needed by the military industry, which must be imported in large quantities, a deep worry appears on the face of this prosperity. Seeking to satisfy needs through military action is an important characteristic of the development history of Japanese capitalism. It's not something that only exists today, but minerals cannot be obtained or extracted in a short period of time. Therefore, the faces of Japanese military industrial capitalists are half ecstatic and half worried.

November 26th

Page 7

Reasons for the Decline in Grain Prices in Zhangzhou and Xiamen: Suspension of Purchases in Taiwan and Shantou 44

Xiamen Correspondence: In the various districts of Southern Fujian, due to the large-scale export of Zhangzhou rice, grain prices have soared. The Zhangzhou authorities, starting from the 9th of this month, have specifically prohibited the export of rice. If the districts of Quanzhou and Xiamen need it, with proper certification confirming that it is for local consumers, it can still be transported. Although Zhangzhou is a rice-producing area, it is only sufficient to supply Quanzhou and Xiamen in addition to its own needs. After this order was implemented, Xiamen rice merchants took the opportunity to manipulate prices. On the 9th, the price of rice per dan (100 market catties) suddenly increased by 5 jiao, which was 1 yuan and 2 jiao 5 fen higher per dan compared to ten days ago. This caused widespread panic. Fortunately, from the 10th to the 12th, 6,834 packages of Zhangzhou rice were successively transported to Xiamen (each package weighing 135 catties). At the same time, rice merchants transported 3,000 packages from Shanghai, with 1,200 packages arriving on the 11th and 12th. The price of rice consequently fell back, from 8 yuan 4 jiao 7 fen per dan to 7 yuan 7 jiao, a decrease of 7 jiao 7 fen compared to three days ago. People's minds were somewhat settled. The reason for the soaring grain prices in Southern Fujian was indeed large-scale exports. There were two destinations: Shantou and Taiwan. The recent purchase of Zhangzhou rice by Taiwan, the first batch successively transported there, was worth over 100,000 yuan, amounting to over 15,000 shi. The second batch purchased was worth over 80,000 yuan, amounting to 12,000 shi. It is said that some of the first batch transported to Taiwan was new rice from the late rice harvest. Due to the rush to transport it, many of the grains were not fully dried and became moldy upon arrival in Taiwan. As a result, Taiwan issued a stop purchase order three days ago to Zhangzhou, halting the transportation of the second batch of rice worth 80,000 yuan. This rice prepared for transport to Taiwan then had no outlet. At the same time, Shantou, having received assistance from Guangzhou, with Xiang rice transported via the Guangdong-Zhangzhou road, saw rice prices plummet. Not only could Zhangzhou rice not profit from being transported to Shantou, but based on Xiamen's high prices three days ago, it was potentially possible to transport rice from Shantou to Xiamen. Thus, the route to Shantou was also blocked. With Zhangzhou rice having lost its two major outlets, it was able to transport over 6,800 packages to Xiamen in three days (the price of Zhangzhou grain has also fallen by 3 to 4 jiao per dan in the past two days). This is the reason for the decline in grain prices. If there is no continued manipulation by rice merchants, it is hoped that the original price can be restored soon (December 13th).

Nanjing Municipal Government Regulates Food Supply: Rice Prices Can Be Stabilized Immediately – Remarks by Mayor Ma 45

Nanjing Correspondence: The Rice Market Management Office, which has been planned for a long time, has had its organizational regulations and grain industry management plans announced. Yesterday, the municipal government formally appointed Zheng Sangshe, the original director of the Rice Market Preparatory Office, as the director. According to the organization, there is supposed to be one more director, but the municipal government, emphasizing practical effectiveness at the initial stage, will prioritize thrift in staffing, so no one has been selected yet. The Management Office is approved to be formally established at the beginning of next week, so that it can engage in the city's grain management in order to balance and regulate the market. Yesterday, the reporter visited Mayor Ma to inquire about his hopes for grain management, methods for smoothly transporting Wuhu rice and grain to Nanjing, and the development of the city's railway expansion and sewer construction projects. Here is a record of Mayor Ma's remarks:

Manage the Rice Market, Stabilize the People's Food Supply

Mayor Ma first said that regarding the establishment of the Rice Market Management Office, although it has been in preparation for quite some time, it is still necessary to emphasize practical work in the future, so that the citizens do not suffer from the pain of soaring food prices. The candidate for director has just been appointed. In the future, matters such as the establishment of warehouses, the investigation of production and sales, the evaluation of prices, and the regulation of grain will be quite complicated, so they should be carefully studied and properly implemented. Mayor Ma's hopes for the Rice Market Management Office are that regulating the people's food supply is a heavy responsibility, and he hopes that all sectors will assist in the process, so that the municipal government and the citizens can work together to establish a solid foundation for the food supply of the people of Nanjing.

Wuhu Rice Transport to Nanjing Can Now Be Smooth

The reporter then asked that since the source of rice and grain from Wuhu to Nanjing has not been smooth, rice prices have risen from time to time. Has the municipal government discussed appropriate measures with Wuhu? Mayor Ma said that Nanjing is not a rice-producing area and has always relied on supplies from other ports. Since the source of rice from Wuhu has decreased, the municipal government has immediately paid attention to this. It has now consulted with Anhui Province and obtained a solution. In the future, when Nanjing purchases rice from Wuhu, the municipal government will issue a sales permit to transport the rice. In this way, the source of rice from Wuhu can be smooth, and the quantity of rice needed in Nanjing can also be statistically determined. The rice price in Nanjing can then be stabilized.

Passenger Trains between Nanjing and Shanghai Will Prepare for Joint Operation

Regarding the city's railway, since its expansion, business has gradually developed. The Ministry of Railways has also responded to the municipal government with a letter expressing its strong approval of the principle of making full use of the city's railway. The city railway is now actively planning to replace sleepers and repair bridge signs, preparing to allow passenger trains between Nanjing and Shanghai to enter the city, so as to benefit the citizens. Mayor Ma said that the Nanjing-Shanghai Railway and the city railway are already connected at Xiaguan in fact. However, the preparations for these passenger trains to enter the city are currently being made to purchase additional vehicles, as the original city railway vehicles are insufficient for scheduling. The stations on Zhongzheng Street in Xiaguan also need to be improved. Therefore, its realization will still require several months of facilities.

Sewer Project Funding Has Been Borrowed

The city's sewer project, from Zhuqiao to Dongguantou, has already begun construction. However, the city's sewer project is extremely arduous, among which the laying of intercepting sewers along both banks of the Qinhuai River is the basic project for the entire city's sewer system and the fundamental method for managing the Qinhuai River. Mayor Ma said that the sewer project from Dongguantou to Shuiximen has been decided to begin construction in January of the 26th year. The total cost of the water project is estimated to be over six million, and about two million is needed in this phase, which the city government has already borrowed and finalized.

"Roundtable Discussions in Beiping" 46

— Special Correspondence from Beiping

The term "roundtable discussion" originated in Japan. Its original purpose is to exchange opinions with each other on a particular issue. Formally, it is more free than a formal conference, and in terms of attitude, it is slightly more serious than a purely private exchange of opinions. Its nature seems similar to the Fabian Society in England and the Saloon in France. However, it is only "similar," and there is nothing more similar than this. In fact, fundamentally, these three each have their own characteristics and are vastly different. For example, the Fabian Society has a strong political party flavor, the saloon has a certain club color, and the roundtable discussion, while accepting the Western-transmitted meeting format, contains a considerable amount of the Eastern style of "waving a duster and engaging in pure conversation" or "gesticulating and talking about world affairs." In short, although all three are lateral expressions of public opinion, their characteristics are inherently British, French, and Eastern.

The existence of roundtable discussions in Beiping dates back several years. However, at that time, roundtable discussions were quite discriminated against by the local authorities, who even regarded them as peripheral organizations of certain action groups. As a result, they were successively ordered to disband by the authorities in various schools. Those organized by social figures were also successively prohibited from holding meetings by the local authorities. Although a few strong-willed people struggled repeatedly and barely managed to hold meetings, they ultimately could not avoid disbanding. The organizers were even arrested. Although most of these arrested organizers were released not long after, they had made promises to the authorities that they would no longer host such roundtable discussions and would no longer be active. Therefore, until November of last year, there were almost no roundtable discussions in this area. The above is the first phase of roundtable discussions here. At that time, the meaning of roundtable discussions contained a certain amount of political elements. The arguments made regarding the promotion of the current society's economic, political, and legal sectors, as well as the review of the international situation, were mostly radical. There was more negative criticism than positive suggestions, and more destructive meaning than constructive meaning. But at the time, the fashion was like this, otherwise it would be misunderstood by everyone. Therefore, from an external perspective, it seemed to contain a certain so-called effect, but after a thorough investigation, most of the participants were simply following the fashion of the time.

Around November of last year, the situation in North China was under further pressure from the Japanese, and the fate of falling into enemy hands was imminent. Traitors and petty villains gathered in the Tianjin and Beiping areas, and Doihara even took up residence in the Fuso Inn (a hotel opened by the Japanese) on Dongdan North Street here. Every day, he would go to the local authorities to urge them to make a decision, claiming that if the plan was not realized, he would never leave Beiping according to the oath he made when he came. A group of frustrated politicians, deposed warlords, and citizens hoping to live in peace followed suit and colluded with the traitors and petty villains to organize groups and openly exchange arguments about willingly surrendering the country. For a time, the situation was very noisy. At that time, anyone with a sense of integrity was heartbroken and tried to express themselves in order to counter these arguments that seemed to be hoping to live in peace but were actually surrendering the country. However, under the circumstances at the time, the former certainly had an overwhelming force against the latter. When the joint declaration of the presidents of various universities and prominent figures in the educational community was first published, it only slightly aroused movement and sympathy on the part of Westerners residing here. In terms of creating a tendency of public opinion, the strength was actually lacking. Therefore, these leaders of the cultural community felt the need to exchange opinions and concentrate arguments with each other. As a result, there were two types of organizations among them, so-called clubs and reunions. In name they were clubs and reunions, but in reality, when everyone gathered, in addition to exchanging opinions on the current situation in order to convey them to the people of the country, petition the authorities, and express themselves to the international community, they only occasionally prepared refreshments or slightly indulged in cigars and cigarettes. Although this did not have the name of a roundtable discussion, it was no different from a roundtable discussion. In addition, there were similar organizations among the teachers and students of various schools, and among the students themselves. But their names were either class meetings, department meetings, or student associations. In fact, all that was discussed was also mostly opinions on the current situation. Sometimes refreshments were prepared, but only to ease the external atmosphere. The reason for not using the name of roundtable discussion was to avoid external associations with the so-called roundtable discussions of the past, and to avoid suspicion. Therefore, the roundtable discussion in this period can be called the second period, which is also the embryonic stage of the roundtable discussion. It had a very great influence on the student demonstrations of the "December 9th" and "December 16th" resolutions.

Last December, the student movement broke out, and for a time the patriotic atmosphere was extremely strong. The arguments of surrender under the guise of maintaining peace were silenced. A group of young students were once again excited by passion, and their actions and deeds often exceeded not only the expectations of the older, more prestigious figures in the academic world, but sometimes even surpassed their own thoughts and beliefs. Because at that time, under the勢 of patriotic fervor, it was impossible to restrain oneself, which was the natural order of things and not at all strange. However, differences inevitably arose in their opinions, and it was almost impossible to exchange them or discuss them. Each person went his own way in what he believed. At the extreme, there was even a tendency to belittle empty talk and emphasize action. Therefore, from last December to January, February, March, etc. of this year, although the student movement was a sensation for a while, continuing one after another, every time a meeting called a roundtable discussion was held, it either ended without results due to mutual shouting and arguing, or one side, which obviously had the advantage, overwhelmed the other, causing them to remain silent. In the terminology popular at that time, this was called giving the other side a blow. Roundtable discussions that lived up to their name only occasionally took place among a few private individuals with similar opinions, and could no longer widely attract the public. This was the stage of formation of the second period of roundtable discussions, because it already had a formal name for roundtable discussions. However, it was also a period of decline, because it had become a mere appendage to action and was no longer of great importance. As for the roundtable discussions in which different opinions could be exchanged without any barriers and gradually create a lateral tendency of public opinion, they no longer existed at this time.

The third stage of the second period of roundtable discussions began after April of this year. At this time, the student movement was strictly prohibited by the authorities, and most of the particularly enthusiastic people were arrested and imprisoned, reaching several hundred people in total. Although they were subsequently released one after another, most of them no longer engaged in the movement. This was one aspect of the situation. Furthermore, at that time, the Japanese were in the process of adjusting the steps of their internal factions. There was the "February 26th" coup and the reorganization of the cabinet internally, and externally there were major changes in the officials stationed in China. There was no time to put direct pressure on the local governments. Therefore, matters that greatly stimulated the feelings of the Chinese people had decreased. Under the circumstances of these two aspects, the action aspect of the student movement had almost come to a standstill. However, the standstill on the action front was precisely what promoted the enthusiasm of all sectors for studying the current situation. As a result, gatherings with the names of lecture meetings, discussion meetings, and research studies, which were no different from roundtable discussions, appeared one after another. At this time, the participants in various gatherings suddenly became enthusiastic. Over the months, social celebrities and teachers from various schools, who had been almost completely isolated from the student community due to differing passions and opinions, gradually began to participate in these gatherings again. Those with radical ideas were also touched by the so-called united front theory that swept the country, and their opinions were slightly restrained. Therefore, the exchange of different opinions and the discussion of matters of common concern gradually became possible. Until September and October, most of these gatherings had adopted the name of roundtable discussion. In November, the outbreak of the Suiyuan War gave the people here near the front line an extremely great stimulus. The Suiyuan support movement flourished for a time and was unparalleled. How to provide assistance was an urgent issue. Therefore, the importance of discussion and the exchange of opinions was also recognized by everyone. As a result, all gatherings of this kind were uniformly called roundtable discussions. When various schools, groups, or circles jointly held such gatherings, there were also so-called expanded roundtable discussions. By this point, the name of roundtable discussion had been universally adopted by social figures. The number of people it netted and the frequency of meetings were even greater than in the first period (that is, before January of last year). It was already commonplace for several large and small roundtable discussions to be held simultaneously throughout the city on the same day. During the previous period of suspension of classes, the gatherings held by social figures, teachers from various schools, and students throughout the city, and also crowned with the name of roundtable discussion, were really more than ten times over. This was the fourth stage of the second period of "roundtable discussions," and also the most prosperous stage since Beiping had so-called roundtable discussions. The issues discussed were mostly directly or indirectly related to the Suiyuan War, and the targets of the exchange of opinions were mostly concrete proposals on how to assist the Suiyuan War.

The second period of roundtable discussions in Beiping has a total of four stages of development. The period it has undergone has been described above. However, the roundtable discussions of the past year are clearly different from the roundtable discussions of several years ago in several points: (1) The latter often contained an internal meaning, with more criticism than suggestions. The former arose under the circumstances of imminent foreign invasion, so the flavor of foreign affairs was strong. When it touched on internal affairs, it was often able to shift direction and strengthen foreign emotions. (2) The latter had a fixed organization, and there were dedicated people responsible. The former was a temporary free gathering, and the conveners were sometimes not fixed. (3) The latter was attended mostly by students and was not adopted by the general public. The former has almost become the necessary form for gatherings in the entire society where various opinions are exchanged and programs are discussed. Although the names are the same, the two cannot be mentioned in the same breath.

Jingdezhen Will Establish a National Kiln Factory: Plans Have Been Drafted by the Pottery Bureau 47

Nanchang Correspondence: The porcelain of Jingdezhen, Jiangxi, in its former heyday, produced 15 million yuan annually. In recent years, it has been completely ruined. The reason for this is nothing more than backward technology and a failure to innovate, resulting in an inability to compete with foreign porcelain. The local authorities of this province, in order to save the porcelain industry, intend to establish a national kiln factory according to the former imperial kiln system, so as to serve as a demonstration and guiding center. This national kiln factory has had its plans drafted by the Pottery Bureau and sent to the Ministry of Industry for review. It is said that the National Economic Construction Movement Committee is urging its establishment. The method is to establish seven factories under the national kiln factory: (1) The Unborn Factory, manufacturing thin-bodied plates, bowls, and the like; (2) The Large Piece Factory, manufacturing bottles, jars, and pots of 300 grades and above; (3) The Pink Decoration Factory, manufacturing bottles, jars, and pots below 300 grades; (4) The Carving and Inlaying Factory, manufacturing various non-circular items; (5) The Blue and White Factory, underglaze decoration; (6) The Colorful Rainbow Factory, overglaze decoration; (7) The Kiln Factory, specializing in firing. The start-up equipment cost for the above is 100,000 yuan, the annual cost is 30,000 yuan, and it can produce 100,650 pieces of porcelain annually.

Shandong Province: Completion of the Library Building and Grand Exhibition of Shanzuo Bronze Inscriptions, Cultural Relics, Books, and Paintings 48

Jinan Dispatch: The Provincial Library, established on the shores of Daming Lake during the late Guangxu period of the Qing Dynasty, was initially housed in a purely old-style building. The pavilions, terraces, flowers, and trees were flourishing, and the originally built picture storage building was grand in scale. However, in recent years, due to lack of repair, seepage and peeling were unavoidable. During the May 3rd Massacre, the building was hit by Japanese artillery fire, with shells piercing the roof. In the summer of the 19th year, the gunpowder depot north of the city exploded, causing further shocks, leading to the sinking of the floors and a precarious state. Furthermore, after the 18th year, the number of books increased, exceeding twice the original collection. Therefore, a plan was made to construct a new building, using 50,000 yuan from the salt license registration fees during Zhang Zongchang's era as a foundation. In the 23rd year, the design was estimated, and construction began in March of the 24th year, and was completed in October, costing over 60,000 yuan. Considering that Kuixing governs Lu and Xuxing governs Qi, the building was named "Kuixu Shucang." Recently, the equipment and layout have finally been completed, and the opening ceremony is scheduled for the 13th of this month. The library has a very rich collection of bronze inscriptions and books. The director, Wang Xiantang, is taking the opportunity of the opening ceremony to hold an exhibition, bringing together collectors of Shanzuo bronze inscriptions, cultural relics, books, and paintings for a grand exhibition. In addition to the bronze inscriptions and cultural relics exhibition room and the Qilu Arts and Literature Exhibition Hall below the building, there is also a calligraphy and painting exhibition. The exhibition will last for ten days from the opening day. The following is a summary of the contents of each section:

Bronze Inscriptions and Cultural Relics Exhibition Room: The room houses bronze ware, jade ware, porcelain, pottery, books, and small stone carvings, all of which are changed from time to time. Collectors also temporarily send hundreds of exhibits, limited to the Shang and Zhou dynasties, not including the Wei, Jin dynasties and later. Among the most famous at home and abroad are various utensils unearthed in Teng County and Yidu, four Zhou Mengshi Dui, Zhou Qibo Meifu Dui, Zhou Zui Dui, Zhou Yuanfu Dui, Zhou Ling Dui, Zhou Jiu Dui, Zhou Shi Yin Gui, Shang Gui Youxing Ding, Shang Gui Youxing Xie, Shang Ni Jue, Zhou Qi Cong Ding, Zhou Qi Cong Zhi, Zhou Qi Cong Gu, Zhou Qi Cong Zhi, Zhou Cong Jue (above are bronze wares), Han Xi Zhong Stone Classics Shang fragments (containing fifty-one characters), Wei Zhengshi Stone Classics Shangshu fragments (containing ten characters).

Qilu Arts and Literature Exhibition Room: It is divided into three sections: books, dictionaries, and rubbings, limited to Shanzuo, also numbering hundreds of items, which are changed from time to time, and borrowed from various collectors. Such as Chen Zhai's Shuowen Jiezi, Jigu Guanyin Kaozheng, Zhai Taowen Shicun, Bao Can Zhai Cang Gu Mu from Weifang, Gao Nanfu Guiyun Ji from Jiaozhou, and landscapes, flowers, grasses, calligraphy and paintings, etc., Wang Yuyang's running script from Xincheng, Liu Shian's regular script and running script from Zhucheng, Zhang Maojun's landscape from Anqiu, Wang Chayou's annotated commentaries on scriptures and portraits, etc., many of which have not been seen outside. There are also many bronze inscription rubbings.

Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition: Antique collectors in Jinan, taking advantage of the opening of the library, have brought out their collections for a centralized public exhibition. Those in charge are Li Jitao, Xin Zhujiu, Kong Jinguang, Huang Xiyue, Xing Zhongcai, Zhuang Zhanyan, etc. They have also borrowed collections from other families, many of which are precious. According to what is known, there is Wang Yan's landscape hanging scroll, worth 3,000 yuan, Song Malin's flower and bird hanging scroll, worth more than 10,000 gold, Qian Chashan's landscape, Shi Tao's landscape and bamboo and stone, Ni Yunlin's landscape, etc., many of which are rare treasures.

Hou Qixiang, a prison official in this county, was dismissed from his post due to a prisoner escape case. Lu Daming, a prison official from Jiading County, was appointed to replace him. Lu had come to Songjiang to take over, but the handover procedures with the previous official had not been completed, so he had not yet taken office. On the evening of the 11th, around 2 o'clock, four serious convicts escaped. It was found that the convicts in Room 18, Wang Asan from Gaoyou, were sentenced to 18 years for extortion, Yang Ada from Gaoyou, was sentenced to 14 years for the same case, Gao Jialun, was sentenced to 14 years for murder, and Fei Liu from Anhui, was a thief who had not yet been sentenced, escaped by breaking through the ceiling and scaling the wall. After the county magistrate received the report, he personally led the army and police to pursue them, but they have not yet been apprehended. Gao Amin and Xu Aba, who were also in Room 18, had their shackles sawed off but did not manage to escape, suggesting a conspiracy. They are currently being interrogated.

Changzhou: Gold and Silver Industry Asks for Tax Exemption 52

Jiang Junli, chairman of the Wuyi Gold and Silver Industry Association, stated that the Ministry of Finance has revised the business tax regulations, increasing the tax rate for silver shops from 10 per mille to 15 per mille, which is unbearable. Yesterday, he specifically sent a joint letter to the Chamber of Commerce, explaining that the business of silver shops has suffered a blow since women started cutting their hair and decorations were affected. Business has plummeted. Furthermore, after the January 28th Incident, the economy has declined, and rural areas are bankrupt. The transactions of silver shops have no room to survive. If the tax rate is further increased, it would be tantamount to kicking someone when they are down. He requested that the Chamber of Commerce forward the request to the Ministry of Finance, urging it to withdraw the order immediately and continue to collect the original amount of 10 per mille. He also requested that the Bureau of Business Tax be notified to temporarily suspend collection until the issue is resolved, in order to alleviate the difficulties of businesses.

Actively Dredging Dongtai Lake 55

Dongtai Lake is a huge flood storage reservoir in Jiangnan and the main source of irrigation. In recent years, it has gradually silted up. Last spring, merchants and others carried out large-scale land reclamation, obstructing the water source and having a huge impact. The project to rectify the waterways is becoming increasingly urgent. In order to actively start dredging work, the Jiangnan Water Conservancy Project Office has specially sent its deputy engineer Cheng Zhenhua and others to survey the area. They will return to the province within days. After Cheng Zhenhua reports the survey situation to the office, the office will formulate a dredging plan based on the plan. According to a person in charge of the office, the Dongtai Lake Dredging Project Office will be established next month, and the personnel are being selected.

Jiaxing: Collection of Land Tax Situation 57

After the Jiaxing County Government sent personnel to compile and investigate the land in the entire county, the tax households have been identified separately. Collection will be carried out in series from the 25th year, and in order to clear the land tax for the year, the land registration staff have been ordered to pursue and urge payment from each household. The county government has also set up collection sub-counters in Xinqiao, Xinfeng, Wangdian, and Wangjiangjing to facilitate the tax payment of grain households. It also telegraphed the provincial department to extend the surcharge period. The surcharges were only levied in accordance with regulations starting from the 11th of this month. According to statistics, as of December 10th, the percentage of grain households who paid the first installment of new tax for the 25th year was more than 60%, totaling more than 500,000 yuan. Efforts are currently being made to urge the remaining households to clear the payment as soon as possible. The second installment of tax will be collected starting from February 1st.

Wuyuan: Expedite the Repair of the Wudewu Highway 60

The Ledewu Highway from Leping to Dewu and from Dewu to Wuyuan were built in the autumn of the 23rd year and the spring of the 24th year, respectively. Although the earthwork bridges and culverts of the two roads have been roughly completed, the road surface has not been paved. Furthermore, due to lack of repair for a long time, the roadbed and bridges have mostly collapsed and silted up, making it impossible to travel. Last month, the three county governments received a face-to-face instruction from Chairman Xiong relayed by the special commissioner's office, ordering the road to be built by a certain date to facilitate transportation. After receiving the order, the Leping area has taken the lead in recruiting strong laborers to repair and build the road, and it has been decided to complete it soon, with a total of more than 40 kilometers of road, more than 20 bridge holes, and more than 10 water pipes to be repaired. The Dewu area is being planned by the county government, but the Wuyuan area needs to raise funds before construction can begin.

Western League Reserve Group: Donghua B Wins the Championship, Winning Lux 2-1 Yesterday for Eight Wins in Eight Games. The Outcome of the Final Game Against the French Chamber of Commerce is Irrelevant to the Overall Situation. 61

Donghua Reserve Group played Lux at Hongkou Park. Because the championship was at stake, the entire Donghua team was cautious. Lux is a strong team and even had players from their A team participating, making their momentum very impressive. After the start of the game, Donghua's Luo Haiguang was late, and they had to play with only ten players. Less than three minutes into the match, Lux's center forward, Ingram, attacked and scored, rolling into the net with an elbow thrust. Lux took the lead. After ten minutes, Luo Haiguang arrived, and the forward line began to coordinate. Ding Zhaocheng shot from 30 yards, cutting across the crossbar into the net, tying the score 1-1. After that, both sides had opportunities but were unsuccessful. As the first half was about to end, Luo Haiguang received assistance from Mai Jiliang and headed the ball from close range, bouncing off a defender into the goal. Donghua took a 2-1 lead in the first half. After halftime, Lux intensified their defense. As the final whistle blew, the score remained 2-1. Donghua won. Since the start of the Reserve Group competition, the order has been brought forward due to good weather. Now it has reached the eighth week. All teams except Lux and Xibu have two games remaining. The rest only have one game left. Donghua has played eight games and won all of them, leading the standings with 16 points, maintaining an undefeated record. Although there is still one game against the French Chamber of Commerce, the outcome is irrelevant to the overall situation because the point difference is three points. Therefore, the championship is already in Donghua's pocket. Although Donghua has given up hope for the A League championship, winning a reserve league championship can also be considered as losing something in the east and finding it in the west.

Billiards B League Competition: Semi-Finals This Week 62

The B League competition held by the Shanghai Amateur Billiards Association has been fierce in the second and third weeks of last week. There were many scoring records exceeding 30 points. The semi-finals will be held this Thursday. Strength Disparity: Jinan Loses to French Chamber of Commerce, Ten to Zero, Five Goals in Each Half 72

The Jinan football team met the French Chamber of Commerce again yesterday at Shenyuan for the second cycle of the Shanghai League A. The Jinan side had a university league championship game with Fudan the day before. After a fierce battle, they had not recovered from fatigue, and their strength was far behind. Therefore, after the contest, the game was spent in a one-sided situation. The entire game only had four or five chances to cross the center line and shoot at the goal, which can be said to be non-existent. Occasionally, there were one or two, but the shots were weak and could not fly over the strict defense lines of Ma Williehart and Bao Saizhong. The general situation of yesterday's game can be included in the above words. As for the progress sequence, after the whistle sounded, the French Chamber of Commerce started the ball. Bao Xiutuo immediately advanced to the baseline and shot far away. Only three minutes later, Roberts Tove opened the scoring. After five minutes, Li Danini headed the ball to make it 2-0. Three minutes later, Roberts Tove came again. Ye saved the danger, but the ball did not fly far. Jemwart took the opportunity and kicked the upper left corner, 3-0. After supporting for a long time, Roberts Tove shot from 12 yards and hit the target, 4-0. After that, Ye Peichu and Guan Zhiyang showed their skills and saved many dangerous balls, but in the first half, Jemwart scored another goal from 15 yards, ending the half with 5-0. Yesterday's game was not because Jinan regressed, but because of the difference between work and rest, and because the strength of the French Chamber of Commerce was much stronger than when they first met.

Shaanxi Province Revises Inspection Methods 76

Shaanxi Province has revised its inspection methods for the 25th year. The province's various education sectors are divided into inspection zones, each with designated personnel. The province is divided into ten school districts: The first school district includes twelve counties such as Chang'an; the second school district includes ten counties such as Dali; the third school district includes ten counties such as Fengxiang; the fourth school district includes eight counties such as Yulin; the fifth school district includes counties such as Suide; the sixth school district includes six counties such as Luochuan; the seventh school district includes seven counties such as Shangxian; the eighth school district includes counties such as Ankang; the ninth school district includes ten counties such as Nanzheng; and the tenth school district includes eight counties such as Xieyang. The inspection methods are as follows: (1) Inspection personnel will, in principle, not be transferred within their designated inspection areas during the school term. (2) Inspectors will adopt a circuit inspection system in areas with relatively convenient transportation, and re-inspect each county at least once per semester, staying for at least five days and no more than fifteen days each time. (3) For the fourth, fifth, eighth, and ninth districts where transportation is inconvenient, one resident inspector should be assigned each semester. The inspector will formulate their inspection plan and itinerary as appropriate and report the inspection results for review.

Overview of Shanghai Municipal Council Schools (7) 86

— Special Report by This Newspaper Hu Zuyin Investigation

Each semester, the school holds parent-teacher conferences, entertainment gatherings, achievement exhibitions, and sports meets, and invites parents to visit the school. Report cards are issued twice each semester, with detailed reports on the children's academic performance, behavior, attendance, and absences. Each school also uses a school-family communication sheet, which is specifically for communication between the school and the family. Every Saturday, the children bring this sheet home for their parents to review, and then bring it back to the school on Monday for the teachers to review. Teachers or parents can sign their opinions or raise questions on the communication sheet so that they can understand or answer each other.

Sometimes, in order to understand the parents' opinions on the school's facilities, the school specifically solicits parents' opinions by printing written questionnaires, asking parents to express their specific opinions on issues such as the school's curriculum, teaching, training, and management. The school authorities collect and compile the opinions of the parents to serve as the basis for improving school affairs. For individual problematic children, the class teachers often visit the children's homes to understand the environment in which the children live and to discuss with the parents the methods of teaching the children.

XIV. Implementation of the Two-Part System

In July of the 23rd year, Mr. Chen Heqin, Director of the Chinese Education Department of the Municipal Council, was sent abroad to Europe to inspect education. Mr. Chen traveled to countries such as England, France, Germany, Italy, Denmark, and the Soviet Union for seven months. Mr. Chen, seeing that the governments of European countries were working hard to promote compulsory education and widely establishing two-part schools to help promote compulsory education (such as in Poland), suggested to the School Affairs Committee of the Municipal Council after returning to China that two-part primary schools be established to promote compulsory education in the concession. This suggestion was adopted by the Municipal Council, and a two-part primary school was first established on Peng Road in February of the 25th year as a preliminary trial.

The two-part primary school is to use full-day school buildings and teachers to divide classes into morning and afternoon shifts to achieve the goal of enrolling twice as many students. There are four classes each morning and afternoon, each class lasting 40 minutes; therefore, each part of the students can take 960 minutes of classes per week. In terms of curriculum, technical subjects such as work, music, and physical education are appropriately reduced according to the number of hours prescribed by the ministry: at the same time, the review work of knowledge subjects such as Chinese, arithmetic, and common sense is designed to allow children to study and do it themselves at home, so as to reduce the time spent practicing in the classroom.

Since the school has been piloting the two-part system, it has not felt any major difficulties in teaching. However, because most of the parents of the school's students work outside during the day, they do not have time to guide and supervise the children's self-study work in the morning or afternoon, so the children's self-study work is inevitably affected to a considerable extent. Another point is that the work undertaken by the school's teachers is more important than the work undertaken by teachers in other schools; on average, each teacher in the school undertakes 1,360 minutes per week, and the student homework that is corrected outside of class is also more than that of teachers in other schools.

XV. Overview of Night Schools

Seeing the plight of apprentices in various factories in the public and community boundaries who are out of school, the Municipal Council first established a male worker night school at the Jingzhou Road Primary School of the Bureau in October of the 23rd year. The worker night school enrolls apprentices working in factories and provides them with considerable remedial education during their spare time. The age of the students is stipulated to be from 12 to 20 years old. The simple courses taught include Chinese, calligraphy, arithmetic, and common sense (including hygiene and citizenship). Later, in order to meet the needs of the students, three elective courses were added: English, singing, and physical education.

When the worker night school was opened, there were a total of 264 students, representing workers from all aspects; the number of people engaged in canning, bookbinding, dyeing, iron industry, light bulb manufacturing, printing, and glass manufacturing was the largest. The number of night school students has increased every semester; by the spring of the 25th year, the number of students had increased to 508. Seeing the development and needs of the night school, the Municipal Council added a female worker night school in February of the 25th year. The school is attached to the Huishan Road East District Girls' Primary School building and specializes in enrolling female workers from various factories in the East District. All facilities are roughly the same as those of the male worker night school. When the school opened, there were 310 students, and it is expected to continue to increase and develop in the future.

After the Xi'an Incident News Reached Shanghai, All Sectors Sent Telegrams Urging Zhang Xueliang 89

Since Zhang Xueliang led his troops in an unusual move and seized Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, the news has shocked all sectors of this city. The Municipal Party Headquarters, the Municipal General Labor Union, the Municipal Farmers' Association, the Municipal Education Association, and various trade associations have all sent telegrams to Zhang Xueliang, urging him to turn back from the precipice as soon as possible and restore Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's freedom, so as not to let the country and the nation suffer. The details are as follows:

Municipal Party Headquarters Telegram

Esteemed Mr. Zhang Hanqing (Zhang Xueliang) of Xi'an, in your esteemed judgment, at this time when foreign enemies are pressing on the border and their advance is directed westward, it is precisely when we should unite internally and resist the enemy together. Now that the good news of the victory in Suiyuan has just arrived and the recovery of lost territories is within sight, you have suddenly taken military action. To say nothing of inviting a thief into the house, which is not permissible by the whole country, the overall national policy cannot be determined by one person. May we ask, if internal strife arises before the foreign enemy is repelled, causing the country to lose its vitality and creating opportunities for the enemy, aiming to resist the enemy in the beginning but ending up aiding the enemy, coming to save the country but leaving with a disaster, what will the world say of you? Our Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has endured hardships and persevered, making painstaking efforts to resist foreign aggression and save the country, planning carefully before taking action. Now that the unity of the country has just been initially achieved and the international status is gradually rising, how can you suddenly shatter the established situation, repeat the fragmentation, cut your feet to fit the shoes, and give others a handle? We fear that before your lost land in the Northeast is recovered, the Northwest will follow the Northeast. Moreover, the hundreds of thousands of soldiers on the front lines are fighting to defend the country, but if they suddenly lose their commander, they will have nowhere to advance or retreat, and will they not be completely placed in a dead end? Considering that you enjoy the special favor of Chairman Chiang and receive generous treatment from the country, you should not bear to make such a rebellious act against national law. We sincerely hope that you will turn back from the precipice, protect the commander, release the troops, and safeguard the overall situation. With utmost anticipation, the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Headquarters bows in respect.

General Labor Union Telegram

Esteemed Mr. Zhang Hanqing of Xi'an, the current international situation is changing rapidly, and China's environment is becoming increasingly perilous. What we seek is China's freedom and equality, and we believe that only by advancing forward as a nation can we strengthen our national power and promote our national prestige. In recent years, the central government has been rectifying national defense and striving for construction, wholeheartedly seeking unity and training the people for self-defense, with painstaking management, all of which are facts. Moreover, the recent dispatch of a large army to slowly suppress bandits is the initial step in launching national policy. If we can take unified steps and obey the central government, then the nation's revival can be expected soon. Unexpectedly, at this critical moment when the front lines are frequently reporting victories and national morale is being promoted, we suddenly heard that your subordinates had taken unusual actions in Lintong and placed Chairman Chiang Kai-shek in a dangerous situation. The more than eight hundred thousand laborers in Shanghai are extremely shocked. The Chairman is the supreme leader of our country, wholeheartedly devoted to saving the country, working tirelessly day and night. He trusts you wholeheartedly and entrusts you with important responsibilities. Although the truth of this incident is not yet clear, we hope that you will promptly and severely punish the rebellious troops, protect the leader, and show the world, preserving your final good name. Otherwise, betraying the country and harming the people will inevitably lead to failure. The lessons of the past are a warning. We hope that you will seriously consider it. The Shanghai General Labor Union bows in respect.

Our Chairman, inheriting this purpose and responsible for its implementation, is all about avoiding the war of internationalism and seeking self-preservation and self-rescue in the process. Now, just as the work of eliminating traitors in Suiyuan is being fought and won, a move to invite a thief into the house has suddenly been made in Shaanxi, destroying the sacred stance and throwing oneself into the embrace of demons, not only repeating the tragic disaster of domestic division but also inviting huge foreign plunder from abroad, being at the mercy of others. Ministry of Industries Issues Order for Adoption of Domestic Litedon Powder; Provincial Government Instructs All Counties to Use as Much as Possible in the Paint Industry to Stop Losses 108

The Shanghai East Asia Paint Industry Factory Co., Ltd., recognizing that China's old-style aluminum powder is made from aluminum nitrate, is explosive and contains toxic substances, which is detrimental to health. The prohibition of its use by domestic laborers is not without reason. The factory's current product, Litedon powder, commonly known as zinc white powder, is made from a mixture of pure zinc and barite. It is of good quality and does not contain toxic components. It is an essential raw material for making paints and rubber, and is indeed a high-quality substitute for white aluminum. It has been chemically tested by the Shanghai Municipal Industrial Testing Institute and issued a certificate. The annual import volume of white pigment Litedon powder is very large. It is a substitute for white aluminum, and the paint industry has already seen results in using imported Litedon powder to replace white aluminum, so there is no need to further promote it and increase imports. Therefore, it is requested that the Ministry of Industries maintain domestic production and issue an order to the social bureaus of all provinces and cities to instruct the paint industry to adopt domestic Litedon powder to stop losses and save rights and interests. Based on this, the Ministry of Industries previously felt that there was a lack of domestic white aluminum substitutes, and advocated temporarily suspending approval of the draft proposal passed by the Third National Labor Congress to prohibit the use of white aluminum in the paint industry. Now, the Litedon powder produced by the company can be a substitute for aluminum, and the domestic paint industry should adopt it as much as possible to promote it. The Ministry of Industries forwarded the order to the province, and in addition to issuing separate orders, specifically instructed the Provincial Department of Construction to instruct all paint industries under its jurisdiction to adopt it. (The company's office is located in Tailai Lane, Maigen Road, Shanghai, and the factory is located in Hengyi West Road, Zhabei, Shanghai.) The Jiangsu Department of Construction, upon receiving the order, submitted a report to the Provincial Government, which yesterday specifically instructed all commissioners and county magistrates to comply.

Establishment of the Siam Branch of the Chinese Medicine Science Society 109

The Bondholders' Meeting of the Tongyi Trust Company Fails; Changed to a Discussion Meeting 110

The Tongyi Trust Company held its third meeting of bank creditors yesterday at 1:00 PM at the Lake Society on Guizhou Road. The attendance of creditors was not enthusiastic. After the meeting started on time, a judge from the Special District Court, acting as chairman, reported that the total number of creditors was over 1,400, with more than 1.6 million yuan owed. However, the total number of attendees was only over 590, representing over 700,300 yuan, which was less than half. Therefore, the meeting was changed to a discussion meeting. The bankruptcy administrator, accountant Li Ding, reported on the liquidation of accounts, and Xu Shihao, a lawyer representing the company's board of directors, reported on the contents of the resumption negotiations and coordination plan. After each creditor expressed their opinions, Judge Wang delivered a speech, stating that the coordination plan required the consent of three-quarters of the total number of creditors to be approved, and the amount of repayment should also be better than the bankruptcy method. It is currently far from the facts and can be temporarily not discussed. As the third resolution to convene a meeting failed, and creditors from other places were unable to attend, it is proposed that the court make a variation and convene meetings separately in various places, pending a ruling. The meeting was then adjourned. A reporter from the Central News Agency learned that the auditors elected by the savings department last Sunday were also requesting the court to interpret the legal quorum. In addition, after the stolen pledged bonds were cashed and the pledged amount was returned, there was still 100,000 yuan remaining, which creditors have strongly demanded to be returned in the short term.

This is hereby announced, including: (1) Second Creditors' Meeting: 2:00 PM on December 17, 25th year of the Republic of China; (2) Location of the Creditors' Meeting: Lake Society, Guizhou Road, Beijing Road, Shanghai; (3) Matters for the Creditors' Meeting: Elect auditors and discuss bankruptcy proceedings.

Fresh Meat Shop Defrauds Goods; Suddenly Declares Liquidation 112

Du Sanzhen Fresh Meat Shop in Nine Acres, opened by a Chaozhou native surnamed Lan, has recently experienced sluggish business. A month ago, the owner of the shop met a runner from the China Cotton Weaving Factory on the road, who said that there were Chaozhou merchants who wanted to purchase large quantities of cotton towels and cotton products for sale in other ports. The runner, attracted by the business, agreed on a price with Lan and delivered the goods to the fresh meat shop, using the Du Sanzhen receipt as proof. The next day, he went to collect the payment and received a check from a bank with a ten-day date, which was cashed in full upon maturity. Since then, the amount of goods traded has been increasing. The latest batch of towels and cotton goods sold was paid for with a check dated the 12th of this month. Unexpectedly, the shop suddenly hired a lawyer last night to announce liquidation and posted a notice asking all creditors to clarify their claims and register at the law office within 14 days for liquidation. The runner from the China Cotton Weaving Factory, believing that Lan should not have used fraudulent means to obtain a large quantity of towels, has hired a lawyer to oppose the liquidation. He demanded that Lan come forward immediately, otherwise he would file a lawsuit in court for fraud and demand compensation for the goods.

Ma Youcai Sues Wife for Adultery; Ma Sunxi Testifies; Xi Daosheng Unable to Appear in Court 113

Ma Youcai, a 32-year-old employee of the tobacco department of the Zhixin Company on Nanjing Road, sued his wife, Ma Gu, 24 years old, who lives at his home in the Ma family house in Chuansha, in the local court, for adultery with his cousin Ma Sunxi, 32 years old (who works as a clerk at the Jiucheng Lumber Company in Xuejiabang). He claimed that due to his work, he did not often return home, which led to his wife having an affair with Ma Sunxi. He was initially unaware of this until he received a letter from Ma Sunxi's wife and based on witness statements from Xi Daosheng, who lived in the same house, claimed to have seen his wife and Ma Sunxi commit adultery in the Sutai Hotel in April, so he requested legal action and filed a private lawsuit for marriage expenses, etc., totaling 1,000 yuan. Ma Sunxi claimed that on April 14th, he came to Shanghai with his wife to visit his uncle and stayed at the Sutai Hotel, which he called a false accusation. His wife, Ma Sun, also went to court to testify that she was illiterate and could not have written a letter to accuse her husband. The letter was written and signed by Xi Daosheng. A fellow villager, Gao Shiyi, also witnessed Xi writing the letter. Ma Gu claimed that her husband had married her as his fourth wife, and all the previous marriages had ended in divorce. Her husband had once said that a wife is like a dish, and you get tired of eating it after a while and need to change flavors, so he fabricated a story to trap her. Judge Xie summoned Xi Daosheng for questioning again. However, yesterday, the defense lawyer stated that Xi had been arrested in Zhenjiang for being a traitor. The judge then declared the debate closed, and the verdict will be announced on the 16th of this month.

Ministry of Communications Rectifies the Shipping Industry; Implements Supervision of Shipping Companies; Stipulates Scheduled and Unscheduled Shipping Routes; Increasing Ships is Based on New Construction in Principle, Restricting Old Ships 114

In order to rectify the shipping industry, the Ministry of Communications, in addition to conducting shipping company registration, has also promulgated supervisory regulations, totaling six chapters and twenty-five articles. The main points are extracted as follows:

Routes

If the number of ships operating on each route exceeds demand, or in special circumstances, the Ministry of Communications may temporarily impose restrictions and establish a route investigation committee to investigate the number and tonnage of ships required on each route. Scheduled ships should be operated by the owner or agent, listing the origin, destination, and stopover ports along the route, and applying to the competent maritime affairs agency to submit to the Ministry of Communications for approval, and a scheduled ship passage certificate will be issued before navigation. If you want to change or suspend navigation, you must still submit it for approval. Unscheduled ships should be operated by the owner or agent to apply to the competent maritime affairs agency and submit it to the Ministry of Communications for approval. The Ministry of Communications will issue an unscheduled ship passage certificate. If unscheduled ships encounter a large number of passengers and goods waiting to be transported on restricted scheduled ship routes, they should first apply to the competent maritime affairs agency for a temporary passage certificate before they can navigate the route. All scheduled ships that are changed to unscheduled ships, or unscheduled ships that are changed to scheduled ships, should apply to the competent maritime affairs agency for approval and report to the Ministry of Communications for record.

Ship Increases

If shipping companies need to increase ships, they should first prepare an application form, attach drawings and explanations, and submit it to the competent maritime affairs agency to the Ministry of Communications for approval. Increasing ships should be based on new construction in principle. If it is an existing ship, in addition to those registered as valid with the Ministry of Communications, the age of passenger ships is limited to less than fifteen years, and the age of cargo ships is limited to less than twenty years. If the original scheduled ships on restricted routes cannot meet the demand, the Ministry of Communications may determine a time limit and order the shipping companies on the route to increase the number of ships within the time limit through the maritime affairs agency. In the event of the circumstances in the preceding paragraph, if the number and tonnage of ships that need to be increased cannot be evenly distributed among the shipping companies on the route, the Ministry of Communications may order mutual consultation to jointly purchase or lease ships for operation. If the consultation fails, the shipping company that can increase better ships may be approved to operate it. In the event of the above circumstances, if the original shipping companies on the route do not increase ships in accordance with the regulations, the Ministry of Communications may order the maritime affairs agency to order other shipping companies to join the route.

Business

Shipping companies should have all colleagues on the same route understand the local passenger and cargo situation, economic conditions, and refer to transportation costs to determine the highest standard for ticket prices and freight rates, once a year, and submit them to the competent maritime affairs agency for approval to the Ministry of Communications. The ticket prices and freight rates of all shipping companies on the route shall not exceed the highest standard. If shipping companies want to jointly operate or share water fees, they should submit them to the Ministry of Communications for approval. Shipping companies shall not distribute profits unless they have made deductions for depreciation and retained public accumulation funds. Shipping companies shall, within two months after the end of each business year, prepare the following forms and submit them to the competent maritime affairs agency for inspection by the Ministry of Communications. The form styles will be determined separately: (1) Employee roster and salary schedule, (2) Passenger and cargo transportation price list, (3) Passenger and cargo transportation statistics, (4) Ship report, (5) Other business reports, (6) Balance sheet of assets and liabilities and profit and loss statement, with explanations, (7) Investigation table of the production and sales of products in various places where ships sail.

Canine Pest Prevention Institute Formulates Guidelines for Prevention and Control of Bovine Plague; Free Treatment of Bovine Plague to Avoid Concerns About Spring Plowing 117

Recently, bovine plague has been discovered in Shanghai, especially among the cattle in the four suburban areas. Therefore, the Jiangwan Animal Plague Prevention Institute in Shanghai has repeatedly dispatched veterinarians to the rural suburbs for diagnosis. The results showed that in addition to arthritis, there were also cases of foot-and-mouth disease. The institute believes that if prevention and control are not carried out quickly, it will affect farming. Therefore, it has issued a notice to all milk farms and farmers in Shanghai to provide free treatment, and has formulated guidelines for the prevention and control of bovine plague to be distributed throughout the suburbs. The details are as follows: Bovine plague is a malignant infectious disease of cattle, which spreads very quickly and causes a large number of cattle deaths, often more than 70-80%. The losses to cattle owners are significant. Therefore, all cattle owners should strictly abide by preventive isolation and disinfection methods to avoid infection and huge losses. Once cattle stop eating, are tired, have an increased body temperature, or a reduced milk supply, they should immediately consult a veterinarian to see if it is bovine plague, so that prevention and control can be carried out. The prevention, treatment, isolation and disinfection of bovine plague are described below: (A) Preventive Injection Methods: There are three preventive injection methods: (1) injection of anti-bovine plague serum, (2) injection of bovine plague organ vaccine, (3) injection of bovine plague serum and toxoid. Each has its own use. If used properly, all can prevent bovine plague. (1) Injection of anti-bovine plague serum is the fastest-acting. It can prevent bovine plague immediately after injection, but the effective period can only protect the cattle for one month. Therefore, after one month, it is necessary to inject anti-bovine plague serum or other preventive fluids to be safe. Cattle herds where bovine plague has already been discovered should be injected with anti-bovine plague serum, especially high-value cattle. (2) Injection of bovine plague organ vaccine takes 14 days to take effect after injection. Therefore, the effect is slightly later than that of anti-bovine plague serum, but the effective period can be six months to one year. Cattle herds that have not developed bovine plague but are at risk of infection should be injected with bovine plague organ vaccine. (3) Bovine plague serum and toxoid are injected at the same time. One cow is injected with two drugs, one is bovine plague toxoid and the other is anti-bovine plague serum. Injecting a small amount of bovine plague toxoid can cause the cow to suffer from plague disease. Injecting a large amount of bovine plague serum can protect the cow from suffering from plague. Therefore, after a cow is injected with two drugs, mild plague is often found and soon recovers. Occasionally, some die from serious illness. All these methods are slightly dangerous, and there are occasional losses. However, cows can be free from plague for one or two years after being injected with this type of injection. This method is best used for cattle herds that have already developed bovine plague, and is not suitable for cattle herds that have not developed bovine plague. When using this method, the entire cattle herd must be completely and simultaneously injected. If a portion is injected and the rest is not, there is a risk of bovine plague transmission. It must not be unknown (B) Treatment Methods: In addition to anti-bovine plague serum, which can treat bovine plague, no other effective drugs have yet been invented. The therapeutic effect of serum is best in the early stages of the disease. Therefore, the earlier the treatment of bovine plague, the better. Serum is also ineffective when the disease is severe. (C) Isolation of Sick Cattle and Disinfection of Cowsheds: Once a sick cow is discovered, it should be immediately isolated for feeding to avoid infecting other healthy cows. It is best to move the healthy cows to a new location and thoroughly disinfect the cowshed where the sick cow was kept. The method of disinfection is to spray the walls and floors of the cowshed with a newly prepared 0.05% bleaching powder solution. The entrances and exits of the cowshed should be covered with lime powder or a disinfectant pool should be set up, containing 5% Lysol, Pysll so that shoes and boots can be disinfected when entering and exiting. All utensils in the sick cow shed must be immersed in a 3% Lysol aqueous solution for 12 or 24 hours, or coated with lime water to kill the residual pathogens. (D) Stop the Transportation of Cattle: During the bovine plague epidemic, cattle must not be moved in or out to reduce the chance of infection. The same applies to other livestock, in order to maintain the safety of the area and prevent the spread of the disease. (E) Prohibit Visits: Because the shoes and boots of visitors are not easily disinfected, they often carry viruses to other places, spreading bovine plague. Visits should be prohibited. Other miscellaneous personnel are also prohibited from entering and exiting the cowshed.
